      function playNextVideo() {
          if (window.__next_video === $('#hs_cos_wrapper_module_1609260709695893 video').length) {
            window.__next_video = 0;
          }
          playVideoAtIndex(window.__next_video);
          window.__next_video++;
        }

        function playVideoAtIndex(index) {
          $('#hs_cos_wrapper_module_1609260709695893 video').each(function(i, video) {
            var $vid = $(video);
            var vid = $vid[0];
            $vid.off('ended');
            $vid.fadeOut('0');
            if (index === i) {
              vid.load();
              vid.play();
              $vid.fadeIn('0');
              $vid.on('ended', playNextVideo);
            }
          });
        }

    playNextVideo();
